href="http://www.amazon.com/review/R2FBNZY17QWNM8/ref=cm_cr_dp_title?ie=UTF8&ASIN=B00P468TMQ&nodeID=672123011&store=shoes"><span class="a-size-base a-text-bold">Comfy, but lacking.</span></a></div><span class="a-color-secondary">         <span class="a-size-normal">     <span class="a-color-secondary">       By     </span>     <a href="/gp/pdp/profile/A32DCJHKUG1KAL/ref=cm_cr_dp_pdp" class="noTextDecoration">D. Huang</a>   </span> <span class="a-declarative" data-action="cr-popup" data-cr-popup="{&quot;width&quot;:340,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;AmazonHelp&quot;,&quot;height&quot;:340}" style="display:inline;"></span><span class="a-color-secondary"> on January 11, 2012</span></span></div><div id="revData-dpReviewsMostHelpfulAUI-R2FBNZY17QWNM8" class="a-row a-spacing-small"><span class="a-size-mini a-color-secondary">Color Name: Black<i class="a-icon a-icon-text-separator"></i></span><span class="a-size-mini a-color-secondary">Size Name: Medium / 9-10 D(M) US<i class="a-icon a-icon-text-separator"></i></span><span class="a-size-mini a-color-state a-text-bold">     Verified Purchase   </span>      <div class="a-section">   I usually wear size 10s and size 9-10 M fit the best for me.<br><br>Pros: Rubber bottom makes it quite durable. Very comfortable and keeps my feet warm.<br><br>Cons: The cushion becomes rather flat really quickly. After wearing these for a few hours a day, the cushion has become noticeably flat after just a month of wear. I also wish it would grip my heel a little more. I'm not a sandal guy and don't like it when my shoes flop around. Size 7.5-8.5 S was definitely too small for me, so that's not the issue.<br><br>If a friend asked me about them, I would tell that friend to buy it, but I wouldn't go out of my way to recommend this product.<br><br>Edit - 2 Years Later - Edit<br>After about 1.5 years of wearing these on a near-daily basis in the winter months, the bottom has started separating from the rest of the sandal. That's pretty much what I expected, so nothing terribly bad there.<br><br>The cushion is pretty much nonexistent now - roughly the equivalent of wearing a pair of socks (or putting on a second layer if you are already wearing socks). I still wear them all the time, mostly for the warmth. </div>  </div>        <a class="a-link-normal comment-link" title="0" They were INCREDIBLE.  I wore them so much (to where they were in shreds!) my wife finally put her foot down and said that if I didn't get rid of them, she would leave. I missed that old gal. Then, when the dirty clothes stopped reappearing after I dumped them in the laundry chute, like they used to, I came to my senses. She's back and the slippers are gone. THESE Acorn slippers are a close approximation to those from EB. Good soles for running outside with the garbage at night. (Keeps her loving me. :)<br>______________<br>edit one year out...<br>______________<br>Well, I should have known that it was too good to last - the slippers, not the marriage.<br>As some others have complained, the seams have given way after about 9 months of use. I am trying to hold out for xmas to get a pair of some other, more reliable brand.  I have been able to add some longevity through the use of gorilla glue. Feels a bit bumpy under my feet though. If any of you know of comfortable and long-lasting slippers, I would appreciate a heads up. thanks. </div>  </div>             <a class="a-link-normal comment-link" title="4" After having them and wearing them most evenings like 9pm to 11pm the sides of both left and right slippers separated from the soles. Rather than bother Amazon about these, I called Acorn. They told me to send them back AT MY EXPENSE,,,, and also $5.00 toward shipping them from Acorn back to me. I said 1st off I don't want to buy slippers every year for something that should last for 5 years or more. They are defective. I was then told to send them and they would decide if they are defective. Save you;re self the aggravation and buy from a more reportable company. I was not going to pay an additional $14 after i spent $32 for the Item because of the defect. It is very clear to me that they were not glued right because that's how they came apart. Right where they were glued.<br><br>I wish i could give them NO starts, But i suppose to the 1 star will represent the comfort of the slippers.<br><br>Cudo's once again to Amazon for helping me again. NO company in the world beats amazons customer service.
